name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr
info:Stayed in April 2024
info:Family
info:3 Reviews
rating:4.7
posted:Posted May 10, 2024
msg:We are a family of four who traveled during the May Day holiday. We chose a lake view room. Two 1.2-meter beds are enough for four people to sleep. The room is very large, the scenery is really beautiful, very close to the lake, it is really cool at night, the floor-to-ceiling windows have screens, there are so many mosquitoes, we dare not open the windows. We came to play during the May Day holiday, it was a bit cool, and it felt a bit cold standing on the balcony at night, so we had to wear long sleeves.
Simply put, we checked in at the end of April, not during the May Day holiday, so the room rate was relatively not expensive, 700-800 per night, and 1,500 yuan per night on the May Day holiday. We drove here by ourselves on our own, and the location of this hotel is really remote. It is recommended to drive or rent a car. Guilin North Station-Hotel, 47 kilometers away, 54 minutes by car, you can imagine how far it is. Since the hotel is built in a place with mountains and water, the geographical location feels like it is next to the mountain. The hotel is very large, and the hotel entrance is quite far from the building where you stay. You must take the hotel car to get there, or drive in by yourself. It is all the scenery of the hotel. It feels beautiful and comfortable to drive around the hotel all the way. We checked in at night and drove in. There was only one registration attendant at the front desk and a little brother who helped with the luggage. No one else. The whole hotel was empty. We checked in on the 29th. There were almost no people staying in the hotel. We didn't see other guests in the hotel. It was very quiet.
The hotel is divided into two areas, ordinary floor hotel rooms and villa area (Guilin Yanshan Songpin Hotel). Both hotels are in this place. It is recommended not to stay in the villa area because there is no lake view, but the garden is not beautiful and the price is very expensive.

Hotel advantages: The hotel environment is five-star, the scenery is really beautiful (take some pictures), if you want to truly experience the mountains and waters of Guilin, you will not regret staying in this hotel. When my baby left, he was very reluctant. The reflection of the mountain in the water is like a picture! The hotel provides a small number of bicycles for three people and two people, so that you can ride bicycles and take pictures in the hotel. (It seems that a three-person bicycle is 98 yuan/hour), check-in also sends the next-door underwater viewing/mobile game park (choose one), and sends three professional photos (with clothing selection). The hotel has Chinese and Western food, both of which are very expensive (tofu is 108 yuan per plate, you can roughly estimate it), and there are also meals delivered to the room (not expensive, 70 yuan per person), the taste is good. It is recommended to choose a hotel with breakfast, not that the breakfast is delicious (because there are no food stores near the hotel). The hotel has complete washing supplies, toothpaste, towels and shower gel. There is a clothes drying rack on the balcony (very considerate), but no hangers. The hotel has to pay for laundry.

Disadvantages of the hotel: If it is not a holiday, there should be few people staying in the hotel, it is empty. There is a swimming pool indoors, but it is not open. It will be open during the May Day holiday (starting from May 1st). There is a small children's playground (that is, the wave pool). It is free to stay and play during normal times, but it will be charged during the May Day holiday (27 yuan per time). During the May Day holiday, you can set off fireworks, which are all hotel activities, and you can also set off water lanterns on the lake. These are activities that are only available during the short holidays. If you go there on weekdays, you really just sleep and look at the scenery. There are no leisure facilities for you. There is only a gym for you to use, and nothing else. Next to the Sunac Amusement Park and Underwater Park, don't have too much fantasy, it's just a very small park, there's nothing fun. If you bring your kids, you must go to the park at 10 am when it opens, and there are basically no entertainment activities in the afternoon. There are almost no food shops near the hotel, don't think about ordering takeout, takeout is very unpalatable and not clean. If you want to eat, you can drive directly to Yangshuo for about 40 minutes to eat. It's best to check in advance for eating in Yangshuo, or check Dazong reviews before choosing. It is recommended to bring some snacks and instant noodles.

In short, if you want to leisurely enjoy the scenery, this hotel is very good, just pure rest and sleep, and then you have to bear with the food and entertainment. If you are traveling to visit attractions, it is recommended to stay in the attractions or the East and West Lanes, so that it is convenient to eat and walk, and it is also close to the attractions. This hotel is really far from the attractions. It's better for you to drive, and it's difficult to take a taxi.
The above is my personal experience, I hope it can help tourists who want to stay.

name:A‚Äçn‚Äçg‚Äçe‚Äçl
info:Stayed in March 2024
info:Family
info:9 Reviews
rating:3.7
posted:Posted March 3, 2024
msg:The three of us settled in the hotel for the Sunac brand. This is our experience and feelings for three days and two nights.
Location and facilities: It is about an hour's drive from the city. To go to urban attractions or eat authentic dishes, you need to go back to the city. The hotel is located in Yanshan District and is worth walking around to appreciate, but it only takes an hour to walk through the entire hotel area.
Lobby reception service: The doorman is very polite and takes the initiative to say hello and help with luggage. The reception staff in the lobby are also very welcoming.
Restaurant service: There is still a lot of room for improvement in service awareness. First of all, the children of our three families are all over 1.2 meters tall, so breakfast requires extra money. Other five-star hotels we stayed in before will take the initiative to waive this fee, but here we will not take the initiative to waive it, and we will keep an eye on every guest for fear of missing something. One of them caused the hotel to suffer huge losses, and when signing for confirmation, the restaurant staff had a stiff attitude; secondly, the uncle who cooked the noodles had a black face and bad temper during the whole process of serving the meal. He did not release the cooked noodles for the guests or Hand it over, but almost throw it out to serve the meal. I have to lament here that these service concepts are still very different from those of old chain five-star hotels.
Room facilities and services: Our requests for services, such as an extra pair of slippers and extra bottles of water, were responded to very quickly. However, the heating effect in one of our rooms was not good. We proposed to change rooms or repairs, but they were rejected. In the end, we were sent two sets of oil heaters.
Supporting entertainment: When staying in the hotel, each room will receive two adult tickets for Happy Tribe or Sea World. Children need to purchase additional UU tickets. However, children's tickets cannot be purchased separately on the mini program. Only adult + child tickets are bundled, and tickets can only be purchased on-site. There were very few people in the off-season. There were only four or five people queuing at the ticket office, but it took a full 40 minutes. The reason is that there is only one ticket window open, and the conductor keeps promoting annual passes. Because one person operates it, the information of previous customers who bought annual passes is also slow to enter into the system, which wastes a lot of time. When it was our turn, we made it clear that we would only buy three children's tickets, and the conductor went out of his way to sell annual passes. Combined with the restaurant service staff's persistence in charging children's breakfast, we all feel that Sunac Sbergh Group puts monetary interests first.
To sum up, these personal experiences have greatly affected the stay experience. This feeling is profound, and from now on I will be skeptical of hotels in all places under the Sunac brand.
